```diff
+import os,sys,shutil
+
+#increase this number for PIP/conda
+PROJECT_VERSION="3.0.8"
+
+this_dir=os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
+
+# ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
+def NewTag():
+	new_version=PROJECT_VERSION.split(".")
+	new_version[2]=str(int(new_version[2])+1)
+	new_version=".".join(new_version)
+	with open(__file__, 'r') as file : content = file.read()
+	content = content.replace('PROJECT_VERSION="{0}"'.format(PROJECT_VERSION), 'PROJECT_VERSION="{0}"'.format(new_version))
+	with open(__file__, 'w') as file: file.write(content)		
+	print(new_version)
+
+# ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
+def DoSetup():
+
+	shutil.rmtree('./build', ignore_errors=True)
+	shutil.rmtree('./dist', ignore_errors=True)
+	shutil.rmtree('./pyplasm.egg-info', ignore_errors=True)
+	shutil.rmtree('./__pycache__', ignore_errors=True)
+	shutil.rmtree('./examples/__pycache__', ignore_errors=True)
+
+	# findFilesInCurrentDirectory
+	def findFilesInCurrentDirectory():
+		ret=[]
+		for dirpath, __dirnames__, filenames in os.walk("."):
+			for filename in filenames:
+				file= os.path.abspath(os.path.join(dirpath, filename))
+				ret.append(file)
+		return ret
+
+	from setuptools import setup
+	is_conda = os.path.exists(os.path.join(sys.prefix, 'conda-meta', 'history'))
+	if is_conda:
+		import conda_build.bdist_conda
+		extra_args={"distclass": conda_build.bdist_conda.CondaDistribution,"conda_buildnum": 1}	
+	else:
+		extra_args={}
+
+	setup(
+		name = "pyplasm",
+		description = "Plasm is a design language for geometric and solid parametric design, developed by the CAD Group at the Universities La Sapienza and Roma Tre in Italy",
+		version=PROJECT_VERSION,
+		url="https://github.com/plasm-language/pyplasm",
+		author="Giorgio Scorzelli",
+		author_email="scorzell@dia.uniroma3.it",
+		packages=["pyplasm"],
+		package_dir={"pyplasm":'.'},
+		package_data={"pyplasm": findFilesInCurrentDirectory()},
+		platforms=['Linux', 'OS-X', 'Windows'],
+		license = "GPL",
+		**extra_args
+	)
+	
+# ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+
+  if len(sys.argv)>=2 and sys.argv[1]=="print-tag":
+    print(PROJECT_VERSION)
+    sys.exit(0)
+	
+  if len(sys.argv)>=2 and sys.argv[1]=="new-tag":
+    NewTag()
+    sys.exit(0)	
+
+  DoSetup()
+  sys.exit(0)	
+
+
```

```diff
+class Utils(object):
+    thisown = property(lambda x: x.this.own(), lambda x, v: x.this.own(v), doc="The membership flag")
+    __repr__ = _swig_repr
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def IsPower2(x):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_IsPower2(x)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Degree2Rad(a):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Degree2Rad(a)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Rad2Degree(a):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Rad2Degree(a)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Clampf(v, a, b):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Clampf(v, a, b)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Clampi(v, a, b):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Clampi(v, a, b)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Overlap1d(__a, __b, __p, __q):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Overlap1d(__a, __b, __p, __q)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Mapf2i(ivalue, ia, ib, fvalue, fa, fb):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Mapf2i(ivalue, ia, ib, fvalue, fa, fb)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Mapi2f(fvalue, fa, fb, ivalue, ia, ib):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Mapi2f(fvalue, fa, fb, ivalue, ia, ib)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Error(*args):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Error(*args)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def Format(*args):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_Format(*args)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def ParseInts(num, dest, string_source, string_format):
+        return _xgepy.Utils_ParseInts(num, dest, string_source, string_format)
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def ParseFloats(num, dest, string_source, string_format):
```
